| `` | `147` | `+        CactusQuantMatrix mat{<br>` |
| `` | `148` | `+            .bits = bits, .K = static_cast<uint32_t>(K), .N = static_cast<uint32_t>(N),<br>` |
| `` | `149` | `+            .group_size = static_cast<uint32_t>(gs), .num_groups = static_cast<uint32_t>(ng),<br>` |
| `` | `150` | `+            .flags = 0,<br>` |
| `` | `151` | `+            .codebook = codebook.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `152` | `+            .input_scale = input_scale.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `153` | `+            .input_scale_recip = input_scale_recip.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `154` | `+            .norms = norms.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `155` | `+            .packed_indices = packed.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `156` | `+            .left_signs = left_signs.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `157` | `+            .right_signs = right_signs.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `158` | `+            .permutation = permutation.data(),<br>` |
| `` | `159` | `+            .rotation = nullptr,<br>` |
| `` | `160` | `+            .expanded = nullptr,<br>` |
| `` | `161` | `+            .norm_f32 = nullptr,<br>` |
| `` | `162` | `+        };<br>` |
| `` | `163` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `164` | `+        std::vector<__fp16> direct(M * N, static_cast<__fp16>(0));<br>` |
| `` | `165` | `+        cactus_quant_matmul(&mat, A.data(), static_cast<uint32_t>(M), direct.data());<br>` |
| `` | `166` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `167` | `+        auto path = std::filesystem::temp_directory_path() /<br>` |
| `` | `168` | `+            ("cactus_graph_cq" + std::to_string(bits) + "_matmul.weights");<br>` |
| `` | `169` | `+        write_test_cq_weights(path, bits, K, N, gs, packed, codebook, input_scale,<br>` |
| `` | `170` | `+                              input_scale_recip, norms, left_signs, right_signs, permutation);<br>` |
| `` | `171` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `172` | `+        CactusGraph g;<br>` |
| `` | `173` | `+        size_t ia = g.input({M, K}, Precision::FP16);<br>` |
| `` | `174` | `+        size_t iw = g.mmap_weights(path.string());<br>` |
| `` | `175` | `+        size_t out = g.matmul(ia, iw, true);<br>` |
| `` | `176` | `+        g.set_input(ia, A.data(), Precision::FP16);<br>` |
| `` | `177` | `+        g.execute();<br>` |
| `` | `178` | `+        __fp16* graph_out = static_cast<__fp16*>(g.get_output(out));<br>` |
| `` | `179` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `180` | `+        bool ok = true;<br>` |
| `` | `181` | `+        for (size_t i = 0; i < M * N; i++) {<br>` |
| `` | `182` | `+            float actual = static_cast<float>(graph_out[i]);<br>` |
| `` | `183` | `+            float expected = static_cast<float>(direct[i]);<br>` |
| `` | `184` | `+            if (!std::isfinite(actual) || std::abs(actual - expected) > 1e-3f) {<br>` |
| `` | `185` | `+                ok = false;<br>` |
| `` | `186` | `+                break;<br>` |
| `` | `187` | `+            }<br>` |
| `` | `188` | `+        }<br>` |
| `` | `189` | `+        g.hard_reset();<br>` |
| `` | `190` | `+        std::filesystem::remove(path);<br>` |
| `` | `191` | `+        if (!ok) return false;<br>` |
| `91` | `192` | `    }<br>` |

| `` | `193` | `+    return true;<br>` |

| `` | `1` | `+# Cactus CQ Pipeline<br>` |
| `` | `2` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `3` | ``+Convert Hugging Face-style checkpoints into Cactus-compatible CQ `.weights`<br>`` |
| `` | `4` | `+directories, then optionally QDQ them back into a PyTorch/HF-style checkpoint for<br>` |
| `` | `5` | `+validation.<br>` |
| `` | `6` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `7` | ``+Run commands from `/workspace`:<br>`` |
| `` | `8` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `9` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `10` | `+export PYTHONPATH=/workspace<br>` |
| `` | `11` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `12` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `13` | ``+Generated artifacts should go under `/workspace/cactus_cq_runs`, not inside this<br>`` |
| `` | `14` | `+source tree.<br>` |
| `` | `15` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `16` | `+## 1. Prepare Calibration Data<br>` |
| `` | `17` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `18` | `+The converter expects a calibration manifest. For best results, use trajectories<br>` |
| `` | `19` | `+generated by the same model family and modality.<br>` |
| `` | `20` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `21` | `+Manifest shape:<br>` |
| `` | `22` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `23` | ```+```json<br>``` |
| `` | `24` | `+{<br>` |
| `` | `25` | `+  "language": {<br>` |
| `` | `26` | `+    "path": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL/language.jsonl"<br>` |
| `` | `27` | `+  },<br>` |
| `` | `28` | `+  "vision": {<br>` |
| `` | `29` | `+    "path": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL/vision.jsonl",<br>` |
| `` | `30` | `+    "base_dir": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL"<br>` |
| `` | `31` | `+  },<br>` |
| `` | `32` | `+  "audio": {<br>` |
| `` | `33` | `+    "path": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL/audio.jsonl",<br>` |
| `` | `34` | `+    "base_dir": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL"<br>` |
| `` | `35` | `+  },<br>` |
| `` | `36` | `+  "transcription": {<br>` |
| `` | `37` | `+    "path": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL/transcription.jsonl",<br>` |
| `` | `38` | `+    "base_dir": "/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL"<br>` |
| `` | `39` | `+  }<br>` |
| `` | `40` | `+}<br>` |
| `` | `41` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `42` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `43` | `+Include only the sections the model actually supports. A text-only model should<br>` |
| `` | `44` | ``+not use a `vision` section.<br>`` |
| `` | `45` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `46` | `+Common row schemas:<br>` |
| `` | `47` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `48` | ``+- Language: `{"prompt_text": "...", "completion_text": "..."}`<br>`` |
| `` | `49` | ``+- Language chat: `{"messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "..."}]}`<br>`` |

| `` | `54` | `+## 2. First Full Conversion<br>` |
| `` | `55` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `56` | `+Use the highest desired precision first and save a Hessian cache. Later lower-bit<br>` |
| `` | `57` | `+variants can reuse this cache and skip calibration forwards.<br>` |
| `` | `58` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `59` | `+### Text-Only Model<br>` |

| `` | `139` | `+    --model-family auto \<br>` |
| `` | `140` | `+    --hessian-cache-in /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/hessian_cache/MODEL_native \<br>` |
| `` | `141` | `+    --force<br>` |
| `` | `142` | `+done<br>` |
| `` | `143` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `144` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `145` | `+VLM lower-language-bit variants with vision fixed at CQ4:<br>` |
| `` | `146` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `147` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `148` | `+for bits in 1 2 3; do<br>` |
| `` | `149` | `+  python -m src.cq_convert convert \<br>` |
| `` | `150` | `+    --model /path/to/hf_vlm \<br>` |
| `` | `151` | `+    --out /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L${bits}V4 \<br>` |
| `` | `152` | `+    --bits 4 \<br>` |
| `` | `153` | `+    --language-bits ${bits} \<br>` |
| `` | `154` | `+    --vision-bits 4 \<br>` |
| `` | `155` | `+    --calibration-manifest /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/native_trajectories_1500_min257/MODEL/calibration_manifest.json \<br>` |
| `` | `156` | `+    --device cuda \<br>` |
| `` | `157` | `+    --model-family auto \<br>` |
| `` | `158` | `+    --hessian-cache-in /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/hessian_cache/MODEL_native \<br>` |
| `` | `159` | `+    --force<br>` |
| `` | `160` | `+done<br>` |
| `` | `161` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `162` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `163` | `+Naming convention:<br>` |
| `` | `164` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `165` | ``+- Text-only: `L1`, `L2`, `L3`, `L4`.<br>`` |
| `` | `166` | ``+- VLM with vision CQ4: `L1V4`, `L2V4`, `L3V4`, `L4V4`.<br>`` |
| `` | `167` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `168` | `+## 4. Inspect The Conversion<br>` |
| `` | `169` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `170` | `+Every output directory should contain:<br>` |
| `` | `171` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `172` | ``+- `.weights` files<br>`` |
| `` | `173` | ``+- `config.txt`<br>`` |
| `` | `174` | `+- tokenizer/runtime files<br>` |
| `` | `175` | ``+- `conversion_manifest.json`<br>`` |
| `` | `176` | ``+- `conversion_summary.json`<br>`` |
| `` | `177` | ``+- `hessian_metadata.json`<br>`` |
| `` | `178` | ``+- optionally `hessians.safetensors`<br>`` |
| `` | `179` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `180` | `+Quick checks:<br>` |
| `` | `181` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `182` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `183` | `+cat /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L4/conversion_summary.json<br>` |
| `` | `184` | `+cat /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L4/hessian_metadata.json<br>` |
| `` | `185` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `186` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `187` | `+Look for:<br>` |
| `` | `188` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `189` | ``+- `unrecognized` should be `0`.<br>`` |
| `` | `190` | ``+- GPTQ targets should have nonzero `hessian_samples`.<br>`` |
| `` | `191` | ``+- `errors` in `hessian_metadata.json` should be empty.<br>`` |
| `` | `192` | `+- Fallbacks should be expected tensors such as norms, positional embeddings, or supported INT8 biases/convs.<br>` |
| `` | `193` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `194` | `+## 5. QDQ For Validation<br>` |
| `` | `195` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `196` | `+Convert a Cactus directory back into a PyTorch/HF-style checkpoint:<br>` |
| `` | `197` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `198` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `199` | `+python -m src.cq_convert qdq \<br>` |
| `` | `200` | `+  /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L4 \<br>` |
| `` | `201` | `+  --out /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L4_qdq_fp16 \<br>` |
| `` | `202` | `+  --model-family auto \<br>` |
| `` | `203` | `+  --force<br>` |
| `` | `204` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `205` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `206` | `+Validate tensor coverage against the source model:<br>` |
| `` | `207` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `208` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `209` | `+python -m src.cq_convert validate \<br>` |
| `` | `210` | `+  --source-model /path/to/hf_model \<br>` |
| `` | `211` | `+  --qdq /workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L4_qdq_fp16 \<br>` |
| `` | `212` | `+  --model-family auto<br>` |
| `` | `213` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `214` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `215` | `+## 6. Package For Cactus<br>` |
| `` | `216` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `217` | `+The runtime package is a zip of the conversion directory. Exclude Hessian files.<br>` |
| `` | `218` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `219` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `220` | `+python - <<'PY'<br>` |
| `` | `221` | `+from pathlib import Path<br>` |
| `` | `222` | `+import zipfile<br>` |
| `` | `223` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `224` | `+src = Path("/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/MODEL_L4")<br>` |
| `` | `225` | `+dst = Path("/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/hf_upload/MODEL/L4.zip")<br>` |
| `` | `226` | `+dst.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)<br>` |
| `` | `227` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `228` | `+with zipfile.ZipFile(dst, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED, compresslevel=6) as zf:<br>` |
| `` | `229` | `+    for p in sorted(src.iterdir()):<br>` |
| `` | `230` | `+        if not p.is_file():<br>` |
| `` | `231` | `+            continue<br>` |
| `` | `232` | `+        if p.name == "hessians.safetensors":<br>` |
| `` | `233` | `+            continue<br>` |
| `` | `234` | `+        info = zipfile.ZipInfo(p.name)<br>` |
| `` | `235` | `+        info.date_time = (1980, 1, 1, 0, 0, 0)<br>` |
| `` | `236` | `+        info.compress_type = zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED<br>` |
| `` | `237` | `+        zf.writestr(info, p.read_bytes())<br>` |
| `` | `238` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `239` | `+print(dst, dst.stat().st_size)<br>` |
| `` | `240` | `+PY<br>` |
| `` | `241` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `242` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `243` | `+Packages must be self-contained. They should include:<br>` |
| `` | `244` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `245` | ``+- `config.txt`<br>`` |
| `` | `246` | ``+- all required `.weights` files<br>`` |
| `` | `247` | ``+- tokenizer files such as `tokenizer.json`, `tokenizer_config.txt`,<br>`` |
| `` | `248` | ``+  `special_tokens.json`, `vocab.txt`, `merges.txt`<br>`` |
| `` | `249` | ``+- `chat_template.jinja2` when the model uses one<br>`` |
| `` | `250` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `251` | ``+Do not include `hessians.safetensors`.<br>`` |
| `` | `252` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `253` | `+## 7. Upload To Hugging Face<br>` |
| `` | `254` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `255` | ```+```bash<br>``` |
| `` | `256` | `+python - <<'PY'<br>` |
| `` | `257` | `+from pathlib import Path<br>` |
| `` | `258` | `+from huggingface_hub import HfApi, create_repo<br>` |
| `` | `259` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `260` | `+repo = "Cactus-Compute/MODEL-cq"<br>` |
| `` | `261` | `+root = Path("/workspace/cactus_cq_runs/hf_upload/MODEL")<br>` |
| `` | `262` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `263` | `+create_repo(repo, repo_type="model", exist_ok=True)<br>` |
| `` | `264` | `+api = HfApi()<br>` |
| `` | `265` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `266` | `+for name in ["L1.zip", "L2.zip", "L3.zip", "L4.zip"]:<br>` |
| `` | `267` | `+    path = root / name<br>` |
| `` | `268` | `+    if path.exists():<br>` |
| `` | `269` | `+        print("uploading", name, path.stat().st_size)<br>` |
| `` | `270` | `+        api.upload_file(<br>` |
| `` | `271` | `+            path_or_fileobj=str(path),<br>` |
| `` | `272` | `+            path_in_repo=name,<br>` |
| `` | `273` | `+            repo_id=repo,<br>` |
| `` | `274` | `+            repo_type="model",<br>` |
| `` | `275` | `+            commit_message=f"Upload {name}",<br>` |
| `` | `276` | `+        )<br>` |
| `` | `277` | `+PY<br>` |
| `` | `278` | ```+```<br>``` |
| `` | `279` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `280` | ``+For VLM packages, upload `L1V4.zip`, `L2V4.zip`, `L3V4.zip`, and `L4V4.zip`<br>`` |
| `` | `281` | `+instead.<br>` |
| `` | `282` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `283` | `+## Practical Notes<br>` |
| `` | `284` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `285` | ``+- Use `--model-family auto` unless auto-detection picks the wrong adapter.<br>`` |
| `` | `286` | ``+- Use explicit `--model-family qwen`, `lfm2`, `gemma4`, `whisper`, `parakeet`,<br>`` |
| `` | `287` | ``+  or `parakeet_tdt` when debugging a known family.<br>`` |
| `` | `288` | `+- Text-only models should not include vision calibration data.<br>` |
| `` | `289` | ``+- A model with no vision tower should not use `V` package names.<br>`` |
| `` | `290` | ``+- Embeddings normally remain CQ4 even in `L1`, `L2`, and `L3` packages.<br>`` |
| `` | `291` | `+- Norm tensors currently remain FP16.<br>` |
| `` | `292` | `+- Bias tensors generally use INT8 where the runtime format supports it.<br>` |
| `` | `293` | ``+- Keep source code in `python/src/cq_convert`; keep generated artifacts<br>`` |
| `` | `294` | ``+  in `/workspace/cactus_cq_runs`.<br>`` |

### [`‎python/src/cq_convert/calibration/loaders.py‎`](https://github.com/cactus-compute/cactus/commit/0f87894bec283c1b051f410acd31bf495312e0e3\#diff-e7c3c3a2d36e177dfcad1aee8a0bb9dbbfca1a83b5962f8a7ec0750d1a74882e)

+55Lines changed: 55 additions & 0 deletions

| Original file line number | Diff line number | Diff line change |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `@@ -0,0 +1,55 @@<br>` |
| `` | `1` | `+from __future__ import annotations<br>` |
| `` | `2` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `3` | `+import json<br>` |
| `` | `4` | `+from pathlib import Path<br>` |
| `` | `5` | `+from typing import Any<br>` |
| `` | `6` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `7` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `8` | `+def read_jsonl(path: str | Path, limit: int | None = None) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:<br>` |
| `` | `9` | `+    rows = []<br>` |
| `` | `10` | `+    with Path(path).open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:<br>` |
| `` | `11` | `+        for line in f:<br>` |
| `` | `12` | `+            line = line.strip()<br>` |
| `` | `13` | `+            if not line:<br>` |
| `` | `14` | `+                continue<br>` |
| `` | `15` | `+            rows.append(json.loads(line))<br>` |
| `` | `16` | `+            if limit is not None and len(rows) >= limit:<br>` |
| `` | `17` | `+                break<br>` |
| `` | `18` | `+    return rows<br>` |
| `` | `19` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `20` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `21` | `+def load_manifest(path: str | Path | None) -> dict[str, Any]:<br>` |
| `` | `22` | `+    if path is None:<br>` |
| `` | `23` | `+        return {}<br>` |
| `` | `24` | `+    with Path(path).open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:<br>` |
| `` | `25` | `+        return json.load(f)<br>` |
| `` | `26` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `27` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `28` | `+def language_text(row: dict[str, Any]) -> str:<br>` |
| `` | `29` | `+    if "messages" in row:<br>` |
| `` | `30` | `+        return "\n".join(f"{m.get('role', 'user')}: {m.get('content', '')}" for m in row["messages"])<br>` |
| `` | `31` | `+    if "prompt_text" in row or "completion_text" in row:<br>` |
| `` | `32` | `+        return (row.get("prompt_text", "") + row.get("completion_text", "")).strip()<br>` |
| `` | `33` | `+    return (row.get("prompt", "") + row.get("completion", "")).strip()<br>` |
| `` | `34` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `35` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `36` | `+def embedding_texts(row: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:<br>` |
| `` | `37` | `+    if "texts" in row:<br>` |
| `` | `38` | `+        return [str(x) for x in row["texts"]]<br>` |
| `` | `39` | `+    if "text" in row:<br>` |
| `` | `40` | `+        return [str(row["text"])]<br>` |
| `` | `41` | `+    return []<br>` |
| `` | `42` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `43` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `44` | `+def load_text_calibration(manifest: dict[str, Any], limits: dict[str, int | None]) -> list[str]:<br>` |
| `` | `45` | `+    texts: list[str] = []<br>` |
| `` | `46` | `+    language = manifest.get("language")<br>` |
| `` | `47` | `+    if language:<br>` |
| `` | `48` | `+        path = language["path"] if isinstance(language, dict) else language<br>` |
| `` | `49` | `+        texts.extend(language_text(r) for r in read_jsonl(path, limits.get("language")))<br>` |
| `` | `50` | `+    embedding = manifest.get("embedding")<br>` |
| `` | `51` | `+    if embedding:<br>` |
| `` | `52` | `+        path = embedding["path"] if isinstance(embedding, dict) else embedding<br>` |
| `` | `53` | `+        for row in read_jsonl(path, limits.get("embedding")):<br>` |
| `` | `54` | `+            texts.extend(embedding_texts(row))<br>` |
| `` | `55` | `+    return [t for t in texts if t]<br>` |

| `` | `24` | `+]<br>` |

| `` | `26` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `27` | `+def copy_runtime_files(model_path: str | Path, out_dir: Path) -> None:<br>` |
| `` | `28` | `+    src_dir = Path(model_path)<br>` |
| `` | `29` | `+    if not src_dir.exists() or not src_dir.is_dir():<br>` |
| `` | `30` | `+        return<br>` |
| `` | `31` | `+    for name in TOKENIZER_FILES:<br>` |
| `` | `32` | `+        src = src_dir / name<br>` |
| `` | `33` | `+        if src.exists():<br>` |
| `` | `34` | `+            shutil.copy2(src, out_dir / name)<br>` |
| `` | `35` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `36` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `37` | `+def write_config_txt(config: dict, out_dir: Path) -> None:<br>` |
| `` | `38` | `+    def fmt(v):<br>` |
| `` | `39` | `+        if isinstance(v, bool):<br>` |
| `` | `40` | `+            return "true" if v else "false"<br>` |
| `` | `41` | `+        if isinstance(v, (list, tuple)):<br>` |
| `` | `42` | `+            return ",".join(str(x) for x in v)<br>` |
| `` | `43` | `+        return str(v)<br>` |
| `` | `44` | `+    with (out_dir / "config.txt").open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:<br>` |
| `` | `45` | `+        for key in sorted(config):<br>` |
| `` | `46` | `+            val = config[key]<br>` |
| `` | `47` | `+            if isinstance(val, (str, int, float, bool, list, tuple)):<br>` |
| `` | `48` | `+                f.write(f"{key}={fmt(val)}\n")<br>` |
| `` | `49` | `+    (out_dir / "hf_config.json").write_text(json.dumps(config, indent=2, sort_keys=True), encoding="utf-8")<br>` |

| `` | `2` | `+<br>` |

| `` | `4` | `+from pathlib import Path<br>` |
| `` | `5` | `+from typing import Any<br>` |
| `` | `6` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `7` | `+import torch<br>` |
| `` | `8` | `+from safetensors.torch import load_file<br>` |
| `` | `9` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `10` | `+from ..model_adapters.adapters import adapter_for_family<br>` |
| `` | `11` | `+from ..model_adapters.detection import detect_family<br>` |
| `` | `12` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `13` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `14` | `+def _dtype_name(dtype) -> str:<br>` |
| `` | `15` | `+    return str(dtype).replace("torch.", "")<br>` |
| `` | `16` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `17` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `18` | `+def _is_integer_dtype(dtype_name: str) -> bool:<br>` |
| `` | `19` | `+    return any(x in dtype_name for x in ("int", "uint", "bool"))<br>` |
| `` | `20` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `21` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `22` | `+def load_safetensor_index(root: Path) -> dict[str, tuple[tuple[int, ...], str]]:<br>` |
| `` | `23` | `+    out: dict[str, tuple[tuple[int, ...], str]] = {}<br>` |
| `` | `24` | `+    for shard in sorted(root.glob("*.safetensors")):<br>` |
| `` | `25` | `+        tensors = load_file(shard)<br>` |
| `` | `26` | `+        for key, tensor in tensors.items():<br>` |
| `` | `27` | `+            out[key] = (tuple(int(x) for x in tensor.shape), _dtype_name(tensor.dtype))<br>` |
| `` | `28` | `+        del tensors<br>` |
| `` | `29` | `+    if out:<br>` |
| `` | `30` | `+        return out<br>` |
| `` | `31` | `+    raise ValueError(f"no safetensors found under {root}")<br>` |
| `` | `32` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `33` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `34` | `+def _state_index(state: dict) -> dict[str, tuple[tuple[int, ...], str]]:<br>` |
| `` | `35` | `+    return {<br>` |
| `` | `36` | `+        key: (tuple(int(x) for x in tensor.shape), _dtype_name(tensor.dtype))<br>` |
| `` | `37` | `+        for key, tensor in state.items()<br>` |
| `` | `38` | `+    }<br>` |
| `` | `39` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `40` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `41` | `+def load_source_state_index(model_path: str | Path, family: str = "auto") -> dict[str, tuple[tuple[int, ...], str]]:<br>` |
| `` | `42` | `+    path = Path(model_path)<br>` |
| `` | `43` | `+    if path.exists() and path.is_dir() and list(path.glob("*.safetensors")):<br>` |
| `` | `44` | `+        source = load_file(sorted(path.glob("*.safetensors"))[0])<br>` |
| `` | `45` | `+        for shard in sorted(path.glob("*.safetensors"))[1:]:<br>` |
| `` | `46` | `+            source.update(load_file(shard))<br>` |
| `` | `47` | `+        if family != "auto":<br>` |
| `` | `48` | `+            source = adapter_for_family(family).normalize_state_dict(source).state_dict<br>` |
| `` | `49` | `+        return _state_index(source)<br>` |
| `` | `50` | `+    try:<br>` |
| `` | `51` | `+        from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModel, AutoModelForCausalLM<br>` |
| `` | `52` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `53` | `+        resolved_family = family<br>` |
| `` | `54` | `+        if resolved_family == "auto":<br>` |
| `` | `55` | `+            try:<br>` |
| `` | `56` | `+                cfg = AutoConfig.from_pretrained(model_path, trust_remote_code=True, local_files_only=path.exists())<br>` |
| `` | `57` | `+                resolved_family = detect_family(cfg, "auto")<br>` |
| `` | `58` | `+            except Exception:<br>` |
| `` | `59` | `+                resolved_family = "generic"<br>` |
| `` | `60` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `61` | `+        try:<br>` |
| `` | `62` | `+            model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_path, torch_dtype=torch.float16, trust_remote_code=True, low_cpu_mem_usage=True)<br>` |
| `` | `63` | `+        except Exception:<br>` |
| `` | `64` | `+            model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_path, torch_dtype=torch.float16, trust_remote_code=True, low_cpu_mem_usage=True)<br>` |
| `` | `65` | `+        state = adapter_for_family(resolved_family).normalize_state_dict(model.state_dict()).state_dict<br>` |
| `` | `66` | `+        return _state_index(state)<br>` |
| `` | `67` | `+    except Exception as exc:<br>` |
| `` | `68` | `+        raise RuntimeError(f"could not load source model state from {model_path}") from exc<br>` |
| `` | `69` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `70` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `71` | `+def validate_qdq(args) -> dict[str, Any]:<br>` |
| `` | `72` | `+    family = getattr(args, "model_family", "auto")<br>` |
| `` | `73` | `+    source = load_source_state_index(args.source_model, family)<br>` |
| `` | `74` | `+    qdq = load_safetensor_index(Path(args.qdq))<br>` |
| `` | `75` | `+    source_keys = set(source)<br>` |
| `` | `76` | `+    qdq_keys = set(qdq)<br>` |
| `` | `77` | `+    missing = sorted(source_keys - qdq_keys)<br>` |
| `` | `78` | `+    extra = sorted(qdq_keys - source_keys)<br>` |
| `` | `79` | `+    shape_mismatches = []<br>` |
| `` | `80` | `+    dtype_mismatches = []<br>` |
| `` | `81` | `+    for key in sorted(source_keys & qdq_keys):<br>` |
| `` | `82` | `+        source_shape, source_dtype = source[key]<br>` |
| `` | `83` | `+        qdq_shape, qdq_dtype = qdq[key]<br>` |
| `` | `84` | `+        if source_shape != qdq_shape:<br>` |
| `` | `85` | `+            shape_mismatches.append({"key": key, "source": list(source_shape), "qdq": list(qdq_shape)})<br>` |
| `` | `86` | `+        if _is_integer_dtype(source_dtype) and source_dtype != qdq_dtype:<br>` |
| `` | `87` | `+            dtype_mismatches.append({"key": key, "source": source_dtype, "qdq": qdq_dtype})<br>` |
| `` | `88` | `+    report = {<br>` |
| `` | `89` | `+        "source_model": str(args.source_model),<br>` |
| `` | `90` | `+        "qdq": str(args.qdq),<br>` |
| `` | `91` | `+        "source_tensors": len(source),<br>` |
| `` | `92` | `+        "qdq_tensors": len(qdq),<br>` |
| `` | `93` | `+        "missing": missing,<br>` |
| `` | `94` | `+        "extra": extra,<br>` |
| `` | `95` | `+        "shape_mismatches": shape_mismatches,<br>` |
| `` | `96` | `+        "dtype_mismatches": dtype_mismatches,<br>` |
| `` | `97` | `+        "ok": not missing and not extra and not shape_mismatches and not dtype_mismatches,<br>` |
| `` | `98` | `+    }<br>` |
| `` | `99` | `+    if args.out:<br>` |
| `` | `100` | `+        Path(args.out).write_text(json.dumps(report, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")<br>` |
| `` | `101` | `+    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2))<br>` |
| `` | `102` | `+    if args.strict and not report["ok"]:<br>` |
| `` | `103` | `+        raise SystemExit(1)<br>` |
| `` | `104` | `+    return report<br>` |

### [`‎python/src/cq_convert/model_adapters/policy.py‎`](https://github.com/cactus-compute/cactus/commit/0f87894bec283c1b051f410acd31bf495312e0e3\#diff-6579b65f7fb047119fa508a41a80e9accde6d4c6ee7cf2067e9a358988b8c7b5)

+47Lines changed: 47 additions & 0 deletions

| Original file line number | Diff line number | Diff line change |

| `@@ -0,0 +1,47 @@<br>` |
| `` | `1` | `+from __future__ import annotations<br>` |
| `` | `2` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `3` | `+from dataclasses import dataclass<br>` |
| `` | `4` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `5` | `+from .naming import NameMatch<br>` |
| `` | `6` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `7` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `8` | `+@dataclass(frozen=True)<br>` |
| `` | `9` | `+class TensorPolicy:<br>` |
| `` | `10` | `+    action: str<br>` |
| `` | `11` | `+    precision: str<br>` |
| `` | `12` | `+    bits: int | None<br>` |
| `` | `13` | `+    component: str<br>` |
| `` | `14` | `+    use_gptq: bool<br>` |
| `` | `15` | `+    rotation: str<br>` |
| `` | `16` | `+    fallback_reason: str | None = None<br>` |
| `` | `17` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `18` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `19` | `+def policy_for_tensor(match: NameMatch, shape: tuple[int, ...], user_bits: int, family: str) -> TensorPolicy:<br>` |
| `` | `20` | `+    component = match.component<br>` |
| `` | `21` | `+    name = match.source_name<br>` |
| `` | `22` | `+    out = match.output_name or ""<br>` |
| `` | `23` | `+    if match.output_name is None:<br>` |
| `` | `24` | `+        return TensorPolicy("ignored", "none", None, component, False, "none", "no output filename")<br>` |
| `` | `25` | `+    if family in {"parakeet", "parakeet_tdt"} and out.endswith(".bias") and (<br>` |
| `` | `26` | `+        "conv_" in out or out.startswith("subsampling_") or out.startswith("ctc_head_")<br>` |
| `` | `27` | `+    ):<br>` |
| `` | `28` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "FP16", None, component, False, "none", "conv bias tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `29` | `+    if name.endswith(".bias") or out.endswith(".bias") or ".bias." in out:<br>` |
| `` | `30` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "INT8", 8, component, False, "none", "bias tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `31` | `+    if family in {"parakeet", "parakeet_tdt"} and "conv_pointwise" in out and len(shape) == 3 and shape[2] == 1:<br>` |
| `` | `32` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "INT8", 8, component, False, "none", "pointwise conv tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `33` | `+    if "conv_depthwise.weights" in out and len(shape) == 3 and shape[1] == 1:<br>` |
| `` | `34` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "INT8", 8, component, False, "none", "depthwise conv tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `35` | `+    if len(shape) != 2:<br>` |
| `` | `36` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "FP16", None, component, False, "none", "non-2d tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `37` | `+    if "position_embedding" in out.lower() or "pos_embed" in out.lower() or "embed_positions" in out.lower():<br>` |
| `` | `38` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "FP16", None, component, False, "none", "position embedding tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `39` | `+    if "norm" in out.lower():<br>` |
| `` | `40` | `+        return TensorPolicy("fallback", "FP16", None, component, False, "none", "norm tensor")<br>` |
| `` | `41` | `+    if family == "gemma4" and name == "model.language_model.embed_tokens_per_layer.weight":<br>` |
| `` | `42` | `+        return TensorPolicy("convert", "CQ2", 2, component, False, "hadamard")<br>` |
| `` | `43` | `+    if component == "embedding" or out in {"token_embeddings.weights", "output_weight.weights"}:<br>` |
| `` | `44` | `+        return TensorPolicy("convert", "CQ4", 4, component, False, "orthogonal")<br>` |
| `` | `45` | `+    if component == "audio" or component == "transcription":<br>` |
| `` | `46` | `+        return TensorPolicy("convert", f"CQ{user_bits}", user_bits, component, False, "hadamard")<br>` |
| `` | `47` | `+    return TensorPolicy("convert", f"CQ{user_bits}", user_bits, component, True, "hadamard")<br>` |

| `` | `24` | `+PRECISION_CQ = {1: 3, 2: 4, 3: 5, 4: 6}<br>` |
| `` | `25` | `+FLAG_ORTHOGONAL_ROTATION = 1 << 1<br>` |

| `` | `27` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `28` | `+@dataclass(frozen=True)<br>` |
| `` | `29` | `+class CQTensor:<br>` |
| `` | `30` | `+    indices: np.ndarray<br>` |
| `` | `31` | `+    norms: np.ndarray<br>` |
| `` | `32` | `+    input_scale: np.ndarray<br>` |

| `` | `34` | `+    group_size: int = GROUP_SIZE<br>` |
| `` | `35` | `+    rotation_family: str = "hadamard"<br>` |
| `` | `36` | `+    seed: int = 1234<br>` |
| `` | `37` | `+    gptq_used: bool = False<br>` |
| `` | `38` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `39` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `40` | `+_CODEBOOK_CACHE: dict[tuple[int, int], np.ndarray] = {}<br>` |
| `` | `41` | `+_HADAMARD_CACHE: dict[tuple[int, int], tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]] = {}<br>` |
| `` | `42` | `+_ORTHO_CACHE: dict[tuple[int, int], np.ndarray] = {}<br>` |
| `` | `43` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `44` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `45` | `+def make_codebook(group_dim: int, bits: int, grid_size: int = 200_001) -> np.ndarray:<br>` |
| `` | `46` | `+    key = (int(group_dim), int(bits))<br>` |
| `` | `47` | `+    if key in _CODEBOOK_CACHE:<br>` |
| `` | `48` | `+        return _CODEBOOK_CACHE[key]<br>` |
| `` | `49` | `+    try:<br>` |
| `` | `50` | `+        from scipy.special import gammaln<br>` |
| `` | `51` | `+    except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover<br>` |
| `` | `52` | `+        raise RuntimeError("scipy is required for CQ codebook generation") from exc<br>` |
| `` | `53` | `+    n_centroids = 1 << bits<br>` |
| `` | `54` | `+    grid = np.linspace(-1.0, 1.0, grid_size, dtype=np.float64)<br>` |
| `` | `55` | `+    log_c = gammaln(group_dim / 2.0) - 0.5 * math.log(math.pi) - gammaln((group_dim - 1.0) / 2.0)<br>` |
| `` | `56` | `+    weights = math.exp(log_c) * np.power(np.clip(1.0 - grid * grid, 0.0, None), (group_dim - 3.0) / 2.0)<br>` |
| `` | `57` | `+    quantiles = np.linspace(0.0, 1.0, n_centroids + 2, dtype=np.float64)[1:-1]<br>` |
| `` | `58` | `+    cum = np.cumsum(weights)<br>` |
| `` | `59` | `+    cum /= cum[-1]<br>` |
| `` | `60` | `+    centroids = np.sort(np.clip(np.interp(quantiles, cum, grid), -1.0, 1.0))<br>` |
| `` | `61` | `+    for _ in range(200):<br>` |
| `` | `62` | `+        bounds = np.concatenate(([-1.0], (centroids[:-1] + centroids[1:]) / 2.0, [1.0]))<br>` |
| `` | `63` | `+        updated = centroids.copy()<br>` |
| `` | `64` | `+        for i in range(n_centroids):<br>` |
| `` | `65` | `+            mask = (grid >= bounds[i]) & (grid <= bounds[i + 1] if i == n_centroids - 1 else grid < bounds[i + 1])<br>` |
| `` | `66` | `+            ws = weights[mask]<br>` |
| `` | `67` | `+            if ws.sum() > 0:<br>` |
| `` | `68` | `+                updated[i] = float((grid[mask] * ws).sum() / ws.sum())<br>` |
| `` | `69` | `+        if np.max(np.abs(updated - centroids)) < 1e-8:<br>` |
| `` | `70` | `+            centroids = updated<br>` |
| `` | `71` | `+            break<br>` |
| `` | `72` | `+        centroids = np.sort(np.clip(updated, -1.0, 1.0))<br>` |
| `` | `73` | `+    _CODEBOOK_CACHE[key] = centroids.astype(np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `74` | `+    return _CODEBOOK_CACHE[key]<br>` |
| `` | `75` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `76` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `77` | `+def make_hadamard_components(group_dim: int, seed: int) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:<br>` |
| `` | `78` | `+    key = (int(group_dim), int(seed))<br>` |
| `` | `79` | `+    if key in _HADAMARD_CACHE:<br>` |
| `` | `80` | `+        return _HADAMARD_CACHE[key]<br>` |
| `` | `81` | `+    if torch is None:  # pragma: no cover<br>` |
| `` | `82` | `+        raise RuntimeError("torch is required for deterministic CQ rotations")<br>` |
| `` | `83` | `+    g = torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(seed + 17 * group_dim)<br>` |
| `` | `84` | `+    left = (2 * torch.randint(0, 2, (group_dim,), generator=g, dtype=torch.int64) - 1).to(torch.int8).numpy()<br>` |
| `` | `85` | `+    right = (2 * torch.randint(0, 2, (group_dim,), generator=g, dtype=torch.int64) - 1).to(torch.int8).numpy()<br>` |
| `` | `86` | `+    perm = torch.randperm(group_dim, generator=g).to(torch.int64).numpy().astype(np.uint32)<br>` |
| `` | `87` | `+    _HADAMARD_CACHE[key] = (left, right, perm)<br>` |
| `` | `88` | `+    return _HADAMARD_CACHE[key]<br>` |
| `` | `89` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `90` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `91` | `+def make_hadamard_matrix(group_dim: int, seed: int) -> np.ndarray:<br>` |
| `` | `92` | `+    try:<br>` |
| `` | `93` | `+        from scipy.linalg import hadamard<br>` |
| `` | `94` | `+    except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover<br>` |
| `` | `95` | `+        raise RuntimeError("scipy is required for Hadamard CQ rotation") from exc<br>` |
| `` | `96` | `+    left, right, perm = make_hadamard_components(group_dim, seed)<br>` |
| `` | `97` | `+    base = hadamard(group_dim, dtype=np.float32) / math.sqrt(group_dim)<br>` |
| `` | `98` | `+    return (left.astype(np.float32)[:, None] * base * right.astype(np.float32)[None, :])[:, perm]<br>` |
| `` | `99` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `100` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `101` | `+def make_orthogonal_rotation(group_dim: int, seed: int) -> np.ndarray:<br>` |
| `` | `102` | `+    key = (int(group_dim), int(seed))<br>` |
| `` | `103` | `+    if key in _ORTHO_CACHE:<br>` |
| `` | `104` | `+        return _ORTHO_CACHE[key]<br>` |
| `` | `105` | `+    if torch is None:  # pragma: no cover<br>` |
| `` | `106` | `+        raise RuntimeError("torch is required for deterministic orthogonal CQ rotations")<br>` |
| `` | `107` | `+    g = torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(seed + 17 * group_dim)<br>` |
| `` | `108` | `+    a = torch.randn(group_dim, group_dim, generator=g)<br>` |
| `` | `109` | `+    q, r = torch.linalg.qr(a, mode="reduced")<br>` |
| `` | `110` | `+    d = torch.sign(torch.diagonal(r))<br>` |
| `` | `111` | `+    d[d == 0] = 1<br>` |
| `` | `112` | `+    _ORTHO_CACHE[key] = (q * d).numpy().astype(np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `113` | `+    return _ORTHO_CACHE[key]<br>` |
| `` | `114` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `115` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `116` | `+def pack_indices_lsb(indices: np.ndarray, group_size: int, bits: int) -> np.ndarray:<br>` |
| `` | `117` | `+    n, k = indices.shape<br>` |
| `` | `118` | `+    if bits == 8:<br>` |
| `` | `119` | `+        return indices.astype(np.uint8, copy=False)<br>` |
| `` | `120` | `+    if not 1 <= bits <= 4:<br>` |
| `` | `121` | `+        raise ValueError(f"bits must be 1..4, got {bits}")<br>` |
| `` | `122` | `+    if k % group_size != 0:<br>` |
| `` | `123` | `+        raise ValueError(f"K={k} is not divisible by group_size={group_size}")<br>` |
| `` | `124` | `+    chunk = 8<br>` |
| `` | `125` | `+    bytes_per_chunk = chunk * bits // 8<br>` |
| `` | `126` | `+    chunks_per_group = group_size // chunk<br>` |
| `` | `127` | `+    grouped = indices.reshape(n, k // group_size, chunks_per_group, chunk).astype(np.uint64)<br>` |
| `` | `128` | `+    word = np.zeros(grouped.shape[:-1], dtype=np.uint64)<br>` |
| `` | `129` | `+    for i in range(chunk):<br>` |
| `` | `130` | `+        word |= grouped[..., i] << (i * bits)<br>` |
| `` | `131` | `+    out = np.zeros(word.shape + (bytes_per_chunk,), dtype=np.uint8)<br>` |
| `` | `132` | `+    for byte in range(bytes_per_chunk):<br>` |
| `` | `133` | `+        out[..., byte] = ((word >> (8 * byte)) & 0xFF).astype(np.uint8)<br>` |
| `` | `134` | `+    return out.reshape(n, k * bits // 8)<br>` |
| `` | `135` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `136` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `137` | `+def _as_numpy_fp32(weight) -> np.ndarray:<br>` |
| `` | `138` | `+    if torch is not None and isinstance(weight, torch.Tensor):<br>` |
| `` | `139` | `+        return weight.detach().float().cpu().numpy()<br>` |
| `` | `140` | `+    return np.asarray(weight, dtype=np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `141` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `142` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `143` | `+def _prepare_input_scale(input_scale: np.ndarray | None, k: int) -> np.ndarray:<br>` |
| `` | `144` | `+    if input_scale is None:<br>` |
| `` | `145` | `+        return np.ones(k, dtype=np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `146` | `+    scale = np.asarray(input_scale, dtype=np.float32).reshape(-1)<br>` |
| `` | `147` | `+    if scale.shape[0] > k:<br>` |
| `` | `148` | `+        scale = scale[:k]<br>` |
| `` | `149` | `+    elif scale.shape[0] < k:<br>` |
| `` | `150` | `+        scale = np.pad(scale, (0, k - scale.shape[0]), constant_values=1.0)<br>` |
| `` | `151` | `+    return np.clip(scale, 1e-8, 65504.0).astype(np.float32, copy=False)<br>` |
| `` | `152` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `153` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `154` | `+def _gptq_correct_group(work: np.ndarray, recon: np.ndarray, h_inv: np.ndarray | None, start: int, stop: int) -> None:<br>` |
| `` | `155` | `+    if h_inv is None or stop >= work.shape[1]:<br>` |
| `` | `156` | `+        return<br>` |
| `` | `157` | `+    try:<br>` |
| `` | `158` | `+        m_bb = h_inv[start:stop, start:stop].astype(np.float32, copy=False)<br>` |
| `` | `159` | `+        m_bs = h_inv[start:stop, stop:].astype(np.float32, copy=False)<br>` |
| `` | `160` | `+        update = np.linalg.solve(m_bb + np.eye(m_bb.shape[0], dtype=np.float32) * 1e-6, m_bs)<br>` |
| `` | `161` | `+        work[:, stop:] -= (work[:, start:stop] - recon) @ update<br>` |
| `` | `162` | `+    except Exception:<br>` |
| `` | `163` | `+        return<br>` |
| `` | `164` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `165` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `166` | `+def quantize_hadamard(<br>` |
| `` | `167` | `+    weight,<br>` |
| `` | `168` | `+    bits: int,<br>` |
| `` | `169` | `+    hessian: np.ndarray | None = None,<br>` |
| `` | `170` | `+    use_gptq: bool = False,<br>` |
| `` | `171` | `+    seed: int = 1234,<br>` |
| `` | `172` | `+    input_scale: np.ndarray | None = None,<br>` |
| `` | `173` | `+) -> CQTensor:<br>` |
| `` | `174` | `+    w = _as_numpy_fp32(weight)<br>` |
| `` | `175` | `+    if w.ndim != 2:<br>` |
| `` | `176` | `+        raise ValueError(f"hadamard CQ requires a 2D tensor, got {w.shape}")<br>` |
| `` | `177` | `+    n, k = w.shape<br>` |
| `` | `178` | `+    original_k = k<br>` |
| `` | `179` | `+    if k % GROUP_SIZE != 0:<br>` |
| `` | `180` | `+        pad = GROUP_SIZE - (k % GROUP_SIZE)<br>` |
| `` | `181` | `+        w = np.pad(w, ((0, 0), (0, pad)), mode="constant")<br>` |
| `` | `182` | `+        k = w.shape[1]<br>` |
| `` | `183` | `+    input_scale = _prepare_input_scale(input_scale, k)<br>` |
| `` | `184` | `+    work = w * input_scale[None, :]<br>` |
| `` | `185` | `+    rot = make_hadamard_matrix(GROUP_SIZE, seed)<br>` |
| `` | `186` | `+    codebook = make_codebook(GROUP_SIZE, bits)<br>` |
| `` | `187` | `+    groups = k // GROUP_SIZE<br>` |
| `` | `188` | `+    indices = np.zeros((n, k), dtype=np.uint8)<br>` |
| `` | `189` | `+    norms = np.zeros((n, groups), dtype=np.float16)<br>` |
| `` | `190` | `+    h_inv = None<br>` |
| `` | `191` | `+    if use_gptq and hessian is not None:<br>` |
| `` | `192` | `+        try:<br>` |
| `` | `193` | `+            h = np.asarray(hessian, dtype=np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `194` | `+            if h.shape[0] == original_k and h.shape[0] == h.shape[1]:<br>` |
| `` | `195` | `+                if original_k != k:<br>` |
| `` | `196` | `+                    h = np.pad(h, ((0, k - original_k), (0, k - original_k)), mode="constant")<br>` |
| `` | `197` | `+                    np.fill_diagonal(h[original_k:, original_k:], 1.0)<br>` |
| `` | `198` | `+                s = np.clip(input_scale.astype(np.float32), 1e-6, None)<br>` |
| `` | `199` | `+                h = h / (s[:, None] * s[None, :])<br>` |
| `` | `200` | `+                h = h + np.eye(h.shape[0], dtype=np.float32) * (0.01 * np.mean(np.diag(h)) + 1e-6)<br>` |
| `` | `201` | `+                h_inv = np.linalg.inv(h)<br>` |
| `` | `202` | `+        except Exception:<br>` |
| `` | `203` | `+            h_inv = None<br>` |
| `` | `204` | `+    for g in range(groups):<br>` |
| `` | `205` | `+        start, stop = g * GROUP_SIZE, (g + 1) * GROUP_SIZE<br>` |
| `` | `206` | `+        group = work[:, start:stop]<br>` |
| `` | `207` | `+        row_norms = np.linalg.norm(group, axis=1).clip(min=1e-8).astype(np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `208` | `+        rotated = (group / row_norms[:, None]) @ rot<br>` |
| `` | `209` | `+        idx = np.abs(rotated[..., None] - codebook[None, None, :]).argmin(axis=-1).astype(np.uint8)<br>` |
| `` | `210` | `+        recon = (codebook[idx] @ rot.T) * row_norms[:, None]<br>` |
| `` | `211` | `+        indices[:, start:stop] = idx<br>` |
| `` | `212` | `+        norms[:, g] = row_norms.astype(np.float16)<br>` |
| `` | `213` | `+        _gptq_correct_group(work, recon, h_inv, start, stop)<br>` |
| `` | `214` | `+    return CQTensor(indices=indices, norms=norms, input_scale=input_scale.astype(np.float16), bits=bits, gptq_used=bool(use_gptq and h_inv is not None))<br>` |
| `` | `215` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `216` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `217` | `+def quantize_orthogonal(weight, bits: int = 4, seed: int = 1234, input_scale: np.ndarray | None = None) -> CQTensor:<br>` |
| `` | `218` | `+    w = _as_numpy_fp32(weight)<br>` |
| `` | `219` | `+    if w.ndim != 2:<br>` |
| `` | `220` | `+        raise ValueError(f"orthogonal CQ requires a 2D tensor, got {w.shape}")<br>` |
| `` | `221` | `+    n, k = w.shape<br>` |
| `` | `222` | `+    input_scale = _prepare_input_scale(input_scale, k)<br>` |
| `` | `223` | `+    work = w * input_scale[None, :]<br>` |
| `` | `224` | `+    rot = make_orthogonal_rotation(k, seed)<br>` |
| `` | `225` | `+    codebook = make_codebook(k, bits)<br>` |
| `` | `226` | `+    norms = np.linalg.norm(work, axis=1).clip(min=1e-8).astype(np.float32)<br>` |
| `` | `227` | `+    indices = np.zeros((n, k), dtype=np.uint8)<br>` |
| `` | `228` | `+    for start in range(0, n, 1024):<br>` |
| `` | `229` | `+        stop = min(start + 1024, n)<br>` |
| `` | `230` | `+        rotated = (work[start:stop] / norms[start:stop, None]) @ rot<br>` |
| `` | `231` | `+        indices[start:stop] = np.abs(rotated[..., None] - codebook[None, None, :]).argmin(axis=-1).astype(np.uint8)<br>` |
| `` | `232` | `+    return CQTensor(indices=indices, norms=norms.astype(np.float16).reshape(n, 1), input_scale=input_scale.astype(np.float16), bits=bits, group_size=k, rotation_family="orthogonal")<br>` |
| `` | `233` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `234` | `+<br>` |
| `` | `235` | `+def write_cq_tensor(out_path: Path, cq: CQTensor) -> None:<br>` |
| `` | `236` | `+    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)<br>` |
| `` | `237` | `+    n, k = cq.indices.shape<br>` |
| `` | `238` | `+    group_size = int(cq.group_size)<br>` |
| `` | `239` | `+    groups = k // group_size<br>` |
| `` | `240` | `+    packed = pack_indices_lsb(cq.indices, group_size, cq.bits)<br>` |
| `` | `241` | `+    codebook = make_codebook(group_size, cq.bits).astype(np.float16)<br>` |
| `` | `242` | `+    input_scale = cq.input_scale.astype(np.float16, copy=False).reshape(k)<br>` |
| `` | `243` | `+    recip = np.minimum(1.0 / np.maximum(input_scale.astype(np.float32), 1e-8), 65504.0).astype(np.float16)<br>` |
| `` | `244` | `+    parts = [codebook.tobytes(), input_scale.tobytes(), recip.tobytes(), cq.norms.astype(np.float16, copy=False).tobytes()]<br>` |
| `` | `245` | `+    flags = 0<br>` |
| `` | `246` | `+    if cq.rotation_family == "orthogonal":<br>` |
| `` | `247` | `+        flags |= FLAG_ORTHOGONAL_ROTATION<br>` |
| `` | `248` | `+        parts.append(make_orthogonal_rotation(group_size, cq.seed).astype(np.float16).tobytes())<br>` |
| `` | `249` | `+    else:<br>` |
| `` | `250` | `+        left, right, perm = make_hadamard_components(group_size, cq.seed)<br>` |
| `` | `251` | `+        parts.extend([left.tobytes(), right.tobytes(), perm.astype("<u4", copy=False).tobytes()])<br>` |
| `` | `252` | `+    scales_blob = b"".join(parts)<br>` |
| `` | `253` | `+    scales_bytes = len(scales_blob)<br>` |
| `` | `254` | `+    data_bytes = packed.size<br>` |
| `` | `255` | `+    scales_end = align_offset(HEADER_SIZE, CACTUS_ALIGNMENT) + scales_bytes<br>` |
| `` | `256` | `+    data_offset = align_offset(scales_end, CACTUS_ALIGNMENT)<br>` |
| `` | `257` | `+    with out_path.open("wb") as f:<br>` |
| `` | `258` | `+        f.write(CACTUS_MAGIC)<br>` |
| `` | `259` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<I", flags))<br>` |
| `` | `260` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<I", CACTUS_ALIGNMENT))<br>` |
| `` | `261` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<I", 2))<br>` |
| `` | `262` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", n))<br>` |
| `` | `263` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", k))<br>` |
| `` | `264` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", 0))<br>` |
| `` | `265` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", 0))<br>` |
| `` | `266` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<I", PRECISION_CQ[cq.bits]))<br>` |
| `` | `267` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", data_bytes))<br>` |
| `` | `268` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", scales_bytes))<br>` |
| `` | `269` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<I", group_size))<br>` |
| `` | `270` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<I", groups))<br>` |
| `` | `271` | `+        f.write(struct.pack("<Q", n))<br>` |
| `` | `272` | `+        f.write(compute_padding(HEADER_SIZE, CACTUS_ALIGNMENT))<br>` |
| `` | `273` | `+        f.write(scales_blob)<br>` |
| `` | `274` | `+        f.write(compute_padding(scales_end, CACTUS_ALIGNMENT))<br>` |
| `` | `275` | `+        f.write(packed.tobytes())<br>` |
| `` | `276` | `+    expected = data_offset + data_bytes<br>` |
| `` | `277` | `+    actual = out_path.stat().st_size<br>` |
| `` | `278` | `+    if actual != expected:<br>` |
| `` | `279` | `+        raise RuntimeError(f"{out_path}: wrote {actual} bytes, expected {expected}")<br>` |
